***orkest.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:orkest.html>orkest</a> (8953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">orchestre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">orchēstra</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὀρχήστρα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">orkhḗstra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὀρχοῦμαι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">orkhoûmai</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (an intensification of <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἔρχομαι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">érkhomai</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go, come</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ergh-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to set in motion, stir up, raise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + suffix *<i>-tra</i> denoting "place".
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">orchestra</span></li></ol>

***ort.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ort.html>ort</a> (68219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:ort.html>ort</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">*orǣt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">that which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> left after eating</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">out-eat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">or-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">eat</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">orte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">refuse of food</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ooraete</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ooreete</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:ort.html>ort</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ort.html>ort</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">urez</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">uräß</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ort.html>ort</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">orts</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fragment; a scrap of leftover food; any remainder; a piece of refuse.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1861</b>,  George Eliot,  chapter III, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:silas.html>Silas</a> Marner</cite>, page 40:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>the rich <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>ate</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:drank.html>drank</a> freely, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="and accepted gout and apoplexy as things that ran mysteriously in respectable families, and the poor thought that the rich were entirely in the right of it to lead a jolly life; besides,">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> their feasting caused a multiplication of <b>orts</b>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> the heirlooms of the poor.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1922</b>,  James Joyce,  <cite>Ulysses</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Come, Kinch, you have eaten all <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> left. <a href = vnd.unilang:ay.html>Ay</a>, I will serve you your <b>orts</b> and offals.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1997</b>,  Thomas Pynchon,  <cite>Mason amp; Dixon</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Peace, Grandam,– reclaim thy <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ort.html>Ort</a></b>. The Learnèd One <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> yet to sink quite that low.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">fragment</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bit</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">chip</span>; See also Thesaurus:piece</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">leftover food</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">gubbins</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">leftover</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">scrap</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">any remainder</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">remnant</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">residue</span>; See also Thesaurus:remainder</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a piece of refuse</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">garbage</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">rubbish</span>; See also Thesaurus:trash</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ort.html>ort</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">orts</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">orting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">orted</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To turn away from with disgust; refuse.</li></ol>
</body>

***oud.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oud.html>oud</a> (505)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">out</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">alt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aldaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*altós</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂eltós</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂el-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grow, nourish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">alt</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">âld</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">old</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">old</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ouderloos.html>ouderloos</a> (125820)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">olderloos</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ouder.html>ouder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">parent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-loos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-less</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ouderloos.html>ouderloos</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">parentless</span>, without any <span class="Latn" lang="en">parent</span>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***over.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> (62)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ōver</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ovar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*uber</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*upér</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*upo</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:ober.html>ober</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_3">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></a>, above</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">postpositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></span> (implying motion)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:kijk.html>Kijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:steekt.html>steekt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:straat.html>straat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>Look out, a dog <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> crossing <b><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></b> the street.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>remaining, left <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>Na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:feest.html>feest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijna.html>bijna</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>After the party there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> barely any food <b>remaining</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>passing by, going away
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>The pain <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>going away</b> again.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>Denotes an imitative action, again, once again,
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schrijf.html>schrijf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brief.html>brief</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></b></i>.
<dl><dd>I will transcribe your letter.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***overal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:overal.html>overal</a> (537)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:overal.html>overal</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:overal.html>overal</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overal.html>overal</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>everywhere, anywhere
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:overal.html>overal</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezocht.html>gezocht</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vinden.html>vinden</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I've looked for him everywhere, but I couldn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> find him.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klein.html>klein</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:overal.html>overal</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:verborgen.html>verborgen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> small, so it could have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> hidden anywhere.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>all <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, throughout (present all <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> a place)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:overbruggen.html>overbruggen</a> (23389)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">over-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bruggen.html>bruggen</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overbruggen.html>overbruggen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bridge, to span</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to connect, to attach</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overcome</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">over-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drijven.html>drijven</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overdrijven.html>overdrijven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to exaggerate, to overstate</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drijven.html>drijven</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overdrijven.html>overdrijven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to float <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p>[A] <b>overdríjven</b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">overgankelijk</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:feiten.html>feiten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groter.html>groter</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kleiner.html>kleiner</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mooier.html>mooier</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:slechter.html>slechter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorstellen.html>voorstellen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>.
